    /**
91 
     * Normalize an angle in a 2&pi; wide interval around a center value.
92 
     * <p>This method has three main uses:</p>
93 
     * <ul>
94 
     *   <li>normalize an angle between 0 and 2&pi;:<br/>
95 
     *       {@code a = MathUtils.normalizeAngle(a, FastMath.PI);}</li>
96 
     *   <li>normalize an angle between -&pi; and +&pi;<br/>
97 
     *       {@code a = MathUtils.normalizeAngle(a, 0.0);}</li>
98 
     *   <li>compute the angle between two defining angular positions:<br>
99 
     *       {@code angle = MathUtils.normalizeAngle(end, start) - start;}</li>
100 
     * </ul>
101 
     * <p>Note that due to numerical accuracy and since &pi; cannot be represented
102 
     * exactly, the result interval is <em>closed</em>, it cannot be half-closed
103 
     * as would be more satisfactory in a purely mathematical view.</p>
104 
     * @param a angle to normalize
105 
     * @param center center of the desired 2&pi; interval for the result
106 
     * @return a-2k&pi; with integer k and center-&pi; &lt;= a-2k&pi; &lt;= center+&pi;
107 
     * @since 1.2
108 
     */
109 
     public static double normalizeAngle(double a, double center) {
110 6 1. normalizeAngle : Replaced double addition with subtraction → KILLED
2. normalizeAngle : Replaced double subtraction with addition → KILLED
3. normalizeAngle : Replaced double division with multiplication → KILLED
4. normalizeAngle : Replaced double multiplication with division → KILLED
5. normalizeAngle : Replaced double subtraction with addition → KILLED
6. normalizeAngle : replaced return of double value with -(x + 1) for org/apache/commons/math3/util/MathUtils::normalizeAngle → KILLED
 
         return a - TWO_PI * FastMath.floor((a + FastMath.PI - center) / TWO_PI);
111 
     }

    /**
136 
     * <p>Reduce {@code |a - offset|} to the primary interval
137 
     * {@code [0, |period|)}.</p>
138 
     *
139 
     * <p>Specifically, the value returned is <br/>
140 
     * {@code a - |period| * floor((a - offset) / |period|) - offset}.</p>
141 
     *
142 
     * <p>If any of the parameters are {@code NaN} or infinite, the result is
143 
     * {@code NaN}.</p>
144 
     *
145 
     * @param a Value to reduce.
146 
     * @param period Period.
147 
     * @param offset Value that will be mapped to {@code 0}.
148 
     * @return the value, within the interval {@code [0 |period|)},
149 
     * that corresponds to {@code a}.
150 
     */

2. reduce : Replaced double division with multiplication → KILLED
3. reduce : Replaced double multiplication with division → KILLED
4. reduce : Replaced double subtraction with addition → KILLED
5. reduce : Replaced double subtraction with addition → KILLED
6. reduce : replaced return of double value with -(x + 1) for org/apache/commons/math3/util/MathUtils::reduce → KILLED
 
        return a - p * FastMath.floor((a - offset) / p) - offset;
156 
    }
